# BMB Mod - Units, Stats & Effects
_SOURCE: Unit definitions_
# Unit definitions
```
// Structure of documents
└── Mods/
    └── Black Market Bazaar/
        └── BMB_Units.xml

```
###  Path: `\Mods\Black Market Bazaar/BMB_Units.xml`

        <Backstory>"I seek no mercenaries; the Silver Swordsmen and their ilk are unwelcome in the ranks of my army. What I seek are heroes - those who wish to make bettering this world their life's adventure!" These words - uttered at the nadir of the Nobles Revolt, when the armies of Procipinee surrounded Relias and his companions at the foot of Mount Essa - remain the rallying cry for all Altar's soldiers. This is an army of adventurers - many of whom are famous in their own right for the quests they have completed - an army that will sometimes dare the impossible and often achieve it.</Backstory>

The commander who would engage this army in battle must possess a similar familiarity with the enchanter's art.</Backstory>

		<Backstory>You remember the binding fire, though Ceresa's rites demand you do not. There were runes carved into the stone of Resoln's oldest temple, and you were pressed against them while the storm gathered overhead. It was not the lightning that changed you, though the lightning came — it was whatever the lightning replaced.

		The woman who screamed during the rites is not the creature that emerged. She felt everything. You feel only the current, and the waiting, and the cold want to let it loose again.

		They call you Tempest Howlers. You do not disagree.</Backstory>

		<Backstory>You remember the passage but not the return. The rite that unmade you in the shadow-places of Resoln was not a rite of death — it only felt that way from the inside. When you crossed the threshold, you were still recognisably yourself.

		When you came back, something came back with you. Something that knows all the doors.

		The living fear you because you are not fully here. You knock against the walls they think can hold you, and the walls open. They call you Intangible Knockers. You pass through regardless.</Backstory>

# Unit stat definitions

// Structure of documents
└── Mods/
    └── Black Market Bazaar/
        └── BMB_UnitStats.xml

<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>
<!-- Black Market Bazaar by Hellions -->
<PlayerAbilityTypes>

    </UnitStatType>
